    }>;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export class CircuitBreaker {
    constructor(config?: CircuitBreakerConfig);
    // (undocumented)
    checkCircuit(endpoint: string): void;
    // (undocumented)
    cleanup(): number;
    // (undocumented)
    getState(endpoint: string): CircuitState;
    // (undocumented)
    getStats(): {
        totalCircuits: number;
        openCircuits: number;
        circuits: Record<string, {
            state: CircuitState;
            failures: number;
        }>;
    };
    // (undocumented)
    recordFailure(endpoint: string, statusCode: number): void;
    // (undocumented)
    recordSuccess(endpoint: string): void;
    // (undocumented)
    reset(endpoint?: string): void;
    // (undocumented)
    shutdown(): void;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface CircuitBreakerConfig {
    // (undocumented)
    failureThreshold?: number;
    // (undocumented)
    halfOpenMaxAttempts?: number;
    // (undocumented)
    resetTimeoutMs?: number;
    // (undocumented)
    staleThresholdMs?: number;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface CircuitBreakerStats {
    // (undocumented)
    circuits: Record<string, {
        state: 'closed' | 'open' | 'half-open';
        failures: number;
    }>;
    // (undocumented)
    openCircuits: number;
    // (undocumented)
    totalCircuits: number;
}

    constructor(endpoint: string, failures: number, retryAfterMs: number);
    // (undocumented)
    readonly endpoint: string;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly failures: number;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly retryAfterMs: number;
}

export type CircuitState = 'closed' | 'open' | 'half-open';

    // (undocumented)

}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface EsiResponse<T> {
    // (undocumented)
    data: T;
    // (undocumented)
    meta: EsiResponseMeta;
}

// @public (undocumented)
function esiResponse<T extends z.ZodTypeAny>(dataSchema: T): z.ZodObject<{
    data: T;
    meta: z.ZodObject<{
        headers: z.ZodRecord<z.ZodString, z.ZodString>;
        fromCache: z.ZodBoolean;
        stale: z.ZodBoolean;
        cacheHitType: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodEnum<{
            "spec-ttl": "spec-ttl";
            "etag-304": "etag-304";
            "stale-on-error": "stale-on-error";
        }>>;
        warning: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodObject<{
            code: z.ZodNumber;
            message: z.ZodString;
        }, z.core.$strip>>;
        requestId: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
        date: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
        contentLanguage: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
        rateLimit: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodObject<{
            remaining: z.ZodNumber;
            limit: z.ZodNumber;
            used: z.ZodNumber;
            group: z.ZodNullable<z.ZodString>;
        }, z.core.$strip>>;
        responseTimeMs: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodNumber>;
    }, z.core.$loose>;
}, z.core.$strip>;

// @public (undocumented)
export type EsiResponseMeta = z.infer<typeof EsiResponseMetaSchema>;

// @public (undocumented)
const EsiResponseMetaSchema: z.ZodObject<{
    headers: z.ZodRecord<z.ZodString, z.ZodString>;
    fromCache: z.ZodBoolean;
    stale: z.ZodBoolean;
    cacheHitType: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodEnum<{
        "spec-ttl": "spec-ttl";
        "etag-304": "etag-304";
        "stale-on-error": "stale-on-error";
    }>>;
    warning: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodObject<{
        code: z.ZodNumber;
        message: z.ZodString;
    }, z.core.$strip>>;
    requestId: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
    date: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
    contentLanguage: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodString>;
    rateLimit: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodObject<{
        remaining: z.ZodNumber;
        limit: z.ZodNumber;
        used: z.ZodNumber;
        group: z.ZodNullable<z.ZodString>;
    }, z.core.$strip>>;
    responseTimeMs: z.ZodOptional<z.ZodNumber>;
}, z.core.$loose>;

// @public (undocumented)
export interface ETagCacheConfig {
    // (undocumented)
    cleanupInterval?: number;
    // (undocumented)
    defaultTtl?: number;
    // (undocumented)
    maxEntries?: number;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export class ETagCacheManager implements ICache {
    constructor(config?: ETagCacheConfig);
    cleanup(): number;
    clear(): void;
    delete(url: string): boolean;
    deleteByPath(pathSegment: string): number;
    // Warning: (ae-forgotten-export) The symbol "CacheEntry" needs to be exported by the entry point index.d.ts
    get(url: string): CacheEntry | null;
    getETag(url: string): string | null;
    getStats(): {
        totalEntries: number;
        maxEntries: number;
        hits: number;
        misses: number;
        hitRate: number;
        oldestEntry: number | null;
        newestEntry: number | null;
    };
    has(url: string): boolean;
    set(url: string, etag: string, data: unknown, headers: Record<string, string>, customTtl?: number): void;
    shutdown(): void;
    updateConfig(newConfig: Partial<ETagCacheConfig>): void;
}

    before?: string | null;
    after?: string | null;
}): Promise<TItem[]>;

export class RateLimiter implements IRateLimiter {

    // (undocumented)
    checkRateLimit(templatePath?: string, method?: string, requestHeaders?: Record<string, string>): Promise<void>;
    // (undocumented)
    getAllGroupStatuses(): Map<string, RateLimitGroupStatus>;
    // (undocumented)
    getGroupStatus(group: string): RateLimitGroupStatus | undefined;
    // (undocumented)
    getStatus(): RateLimitInfo;
    // (undocumented)
    static getTokenCost(statusCode: number): number;
    // (undocumented)
    isBlocked(group?: string): boolean;
    // (undocumented)
    reset(): void;
    // (undocumented)
    setTestMode(enabled: boolean): void;
    // (undocumented)
    updateFromResponse(headers: Record<string, string>, statusCode: number, templatePath?: string, method?: string, requestHeaders?: Record<string, string>): void;
    // (undocumented)
    updateRateLimitInfo(headers: Record<string, string>): void;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export type WithMetadata<T> = {
    [K in keyof T]: T[K] extends (...args: infer A) => Promise<infer R> ? (...args: A) => Promise<EsiResponse<R>> : T[K];
};
